# 2
U: what is drake's most popular song ?
UT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
UT: sort(popularity desc of @org.thingpedia.media-source.song() filter contains(artists, null^^org.thingpedia.media-source:artist("drake")))[1];
C: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
C: sort(popularity desc of @org.thingpedia.media-source(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).song() filter contains(artists, "spotify:artist:3TVXtAsR1Inumwj472S9r4"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:artist("Drake")))[1]
C: #[results=[
C:   { id="spotify:track:127QTOFJsJQp5LbJbu3A1y"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Toosie Slide"), artists=["spotify:artist:3TVXtAsR1Inumwj472S9r4"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:artist("Drake")], release_date=new Date("2020-04-03T00:00:00.000Z"), popularity=93, energy=45, danceability=83 }
C: ]];
A: his most popular song right now is toosie slide . would you like to play this song ?
AT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.sys_recommend_one;
AT: @org.thingpedia.media-player(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).play(playable="spotify:track:127QTOFJsJQp5LbJbu3A1y"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Toosie Slide"))
AT: #[confirm=enum proposed];
U: i don't know that song . when was it released ?
UT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
UT: [release_date] of sort(popularity desc of @org.thingpedia.media-source(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).song() filter contains(artists, "spotify:artist:3TVXtAsR1Inumwj472S9r4"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:artist("Drake")) && id == "spotify:track:127QTOFJsJQp5LbJbu3A1y"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Toosie Slide"))[1];
C: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
C: sort(popularity desc of @org.thingpedia.media-source(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).song() filter contains(artists, "spotify:artist:3TVXtAsR1Inumwj472S9r4"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:artist("Drake")))[1]
C: #[results=[
C:   { id="spotify:track:127QTOFJsJQp5LbJbu3A1y"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Toosie Slide"), artists=["spotify:artist:3TVXtAsR1Inumwj472S9r4"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:artist("Drake")], release_date=new Date("2020-04-03T00:00:00.000Z"), popularity=93, energy=45, danceability=83 }
C: ]];
C: [release_date] of sort(popularity desc of @org.thingpedia.media-source(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).song() filter contains(artists, "spotify:artist:3TVXtAsR1Inumwj472S9r4"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:artist("Drake")) && id == "spotify:track:127QTOFJsJQp5LbJbu3A1y"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Toosie Slide"))[1]
C: #[results=[
C:   { id="spotify:track:127QTOFJsJQp5LbJbu3A1y"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Toosie Slide"), release_date=new Date("2020-04-03T00:00:00.000Z") }
C: ]];
A: toosie slide was released on april 3rd 2020 .
AT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.sys_recommend_one;
U: ok thanks, goodbye .
UT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.cancel;

# 5
U: hi, i'm having a party later would the song despacito be good for dancing .
UT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
UT: [danceability] of @org.thingpedia.media-source.song() filter id =~ "despacito";
C: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
C: [danceability] of @org.thingpedia.media-source(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).song() filter id =~ "despacito"
C: #[results=[
C:   { id="spotify:track:6habFhsOp2NvshLv26DqMb"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Despacito"), danceability=65 }
C: ]];
A: the danceability is 65 out of 100 . would you like me to play this song ?
AT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.sys_recommend_one;
AT: @org.thingpedia.media-player(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).play(playable="spotify:track:6habFhsOp2NvshLv26DqMb"^^org.thingpedia.media-source:song("Despacito"))
AT: #[confirm=enum proposed];
U: no thank you, maybe later .
UT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.cancel;

U: can you play some weird music from the noise genre
UT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
UT: @org.thingpedia.media-source.playable() filter contains~(genres, "noise") => @org.thingpedia.media-player.play(playable=id);

UT: sort(release_date desc of @org.thingpedia.media-source.song() filter release_date <= new Date("1970-01-01T08:00:00.000Z") + 1year && release_date >= new Date("1970-01-01T08:00:00.000Z"))[1] => @org.thingpedia.media-player.play(playable=id);

UT: sort(popularity desc of @org.thingpedia.media-source.song() filter release_date <= new Date("2015-01-01T08:00:00.000Z") + 1year && release_date >= new Date("2015-01-01T08:00:00.000Z"))[1 : 20] => @org.thingpedia.media-player.play(playable=id);
====

U: create playlist
UT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.execute;
UT: @com.spotify.create_playlist();

C: @com.spotify(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).create_playlist();

AT: $dialogue @org.thingpedia.dialogue.transaction.sys_slot_fill(name);
AT: @com.spotify(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).create_playlist();

UT: @com.spotify(id="com.spotify-XXXXXXXX"^^tt:device_id).create_playlist(name="one");
